<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смывать.html>смыва́ть</a> (12829)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смыть.html>смыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смывать.html>смыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smyvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смыть.html>смыть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash off, to flush</li>
<li>to wash away, to wash down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смывать.html>смыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smyvátʹ</b> volnój s súdna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wash overboard</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">lofty</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wash away, to redeem, to atone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смывать.html>смыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грех.html>грехи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молитва.html>моли́твой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smyvátʹ</b> grexí molítvoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pray to wash away one's sins</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смыкаться.html>смыка́ться</a> (15304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смыкать.html>смыка́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smykátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смыкаться.html>смыка́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smykátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сомкнуться.html>сомкну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to close <i>(up)</i>, to close down <i>(upon)</i>, to close in <i>(on)</i>, <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to close</li>
<li>to close

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мыслить.html>мы́слить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mýslitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смыслить.html>смы́слить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smýslitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to understand</li>
<li>to be knowledgeable <i>(about)</i>, to know something <i>(about)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ухо.html>уха</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыло.html>ры́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смыслить.html>смы́слить</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni uxa ni rýla ne smýslitʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not to know beans <i>(about)</i>; not to understand a damn thing <i>(about)</i></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мыть.html>мыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смыть.html>смыть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смывать.html>смыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to wash off, to flush</li>
<li>to wash away, to wash down
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смыть.html>смыть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smytʹ</b> volnój s súdna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wash overboard</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">lofty</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wash away, to redeem, to atone
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смыть.html>смыть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:грех.html>грехи́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:молитва.html>моли́твой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>smytʹ</b> grexí molítvoj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to pray to wash away one's sins</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">смык</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smyk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">смичо́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smyčók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жало.html>смычо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smyčók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смычок.html>смычка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смычок.html>смычки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смычок.html>смычко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>fiddlestick, bow <i>(rod used for playing stringed instruments)</i></li></ol>

<p><b>смыш<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>лё<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мышл-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ён</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчить.html>смягчи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smjaxčítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчать.html>смягча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smjaxčátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчить.html>смягчи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soften, to extenuate</li>
<li>to allay, to assuage, to mitigate, to alleviate</li>
<li>to tone down <i>light, colors</i></li>
<li>to relax <i>harshness</i></li>
<li>to mollify</li>
<li>to palatalize</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчаться.html>смягча́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smjaxčátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчиться.html>смягчи́ться</a></b>)

<li>to relent, to soften, to grow lenient</li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчение.html>смягче́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smjaxčénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчение.html>смягче́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчение.html>смягче́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчение.html>смягче́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mitigation, palliation</li>
<li>softening</li>
<li>alleviation, relief, assuagement</li>
<li>abatement</li>
<li>mollification</li>
<li>palatalization</li>
<li>give</li>
<li>easing off</li></ol>

***смягчить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смягчить.html>смягчи́ть</a> (11607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjáxkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчить.html>смягчи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smjaxčítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчать.html>смягча́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soften extenuate</li>
<li>to allay, to assuage, to mitigate, to alleviate</li>
<li>to tone down <i>light, colors</i></li>
<li>to relax <i>harshness</i></li>
<li>to mollify</li>
<li>to palatalize</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчить.html>смягчи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smjaxčítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчиться.html>смягчи́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smjaxčítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчаться.html>смягча́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to soften, to become soft(er)</li>
<li>to relent, to soften, to grow lenient</li>
<li>to ease <i>(off)</i>, to lessen, <i>(wind)</i> to relent</li>
<li><i>(weather)</i> to grow mild(er)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смягчить.html>смягчи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">smjaxčítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***смятение.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смятение.html>смяте́ние</a> (9980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смятение.html>смяте́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smjaténije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смятение.html>смяте́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смятение.html>смяте́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смятение.html>смяте́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>confusion, disarray, tizzy</li>
<li>turmoil, agitation</li>
<li>tumult</li>
<li>commotion, whirl</li>
<li>perturbation</li>
<li>dither</li>
<li>alarm <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">sudden surprise with fear or terror</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>distraction</li></ol>

<p><b>смя<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>те́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>е</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:смять.html>смять</a> (6787)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смять.html>смять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">smjatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сминать.html>смина́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rumple, to crumple, to wrinkle, to fumble, to crease</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:смять.html>смять</a></b>

Зализняка — 14*b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующие</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́лы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:мять.html>мять</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сминать.html>смина́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b>с-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-мя-</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
